            <div class="Grid-col">
             <h2 class="heading-a font-semibold">
              About this item
             </h2>
            </div>
            <div class="Grid-col u-size-11-12">
             <p class="about-item-preview-text js-about-item-preview-text">
              Enjoy a new look to the classic game of Monopoly in this USAopoly Monopoly Board Game. It has a post-apocalyptic setting with an eerie feel perfect for game night around Halloween or any time. It adds a zombie twist to the classic holiday game. This Walking Dead board game, "Survival Edition," features six tokens to match the theme. It also provides an optional speed play for shorter games. You are guaranteed a fight to the finish regardless of which method of play you choose. This game will keep you and your guests entertained all evening long as you battle to see who is the last zombie left standing. This is a fun version for any true Monopoly fan.
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="Grid-col u-size-1-12 hide-content-m">

            <h2 class="heading-a">
             About this item
            </h2>
            <section class="product-about js-about-item">
             <section class="js-legal-badges legal-badges">
              <div class="js-idml-badge legal-badge Grid">
               <div class="legal-image Grid-col u-size-2-12 u-size-3-12-xs u-size-2-12-s">
                <img alt="" src="http://ll-us-i5.wal.co/dfw/63fd9f59-82e4/k2-_8d6d245e-2878-4468-a829-5a4ac12350ad.v1.png-34dd6279f37128a51da67be1bc3d2191bebf70ec-crushed-60x60.png"/>

             <div class="js-ellipsis module" data-max-height="350">
              <p>
               Enjoy a new look to the classic game of Monopoly in this USAopoly Monopoly Board Game. It has a post-apocalyptic setting with an eerie feel perfect for game night around Halloween or any time. It adds a zombie twist to the classic holiday game. This Walking Dead board game, "Survival Edition," features six tokens to match the theme. It also provides an optional speed play for shorter games. You are guaranteed a fight to the finish regardless of which method of play you choose. This game will keep you and your guests entertained all evening long as you battle to see who is the last zombie left standing. This is a fun version for any true Monopoly fan.
              </p>
              <p>
               <br/>
               <b>
                USAopoly Monopoly: Walking Dead "Survival Edition" Game:
               </b>
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Adult board games are designed for 2 to 6 players
               </li>
               <li>
                Classic Monopoly play with a zombie twist
               </li>
               <li>
                Speed play option
               </li>
               <li>
                6 collectible Walking Dead-themed tokens
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
              </p>

                  <p class="js-customer-review-text" data-max-height="110">
                   My family just loved this special edition of monopoly in the walking dead version. Money is represented as inventory such as weapons, gas, ammo,bags of seeds exc. transportation is horse, motorcycle, rv, truck. Instead of income tax you pay for protection. Community chest &amp; chance are now supply chest &amp; scavenge. Utilities are bottled water &amp; battery. Great game for all especially for the walking dead fan.
                  </p>
